EXPLANATORY NOTE</font></p>
<p style=

<a name="_DV_C10" id="_DV_C10"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none;">This
Amendment No. 1 on Form 10-K/A (this “Amendment”) amends Reading
International, Inc.’s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 , originally filed with the Securities and
Exchange Commission, or SEC, on March&nbsp;16, 2018&nbsp;&nbsp;(the
“Original Filing”). We are amending and refiling Part III to
include information required by Items 10, 11, 12, 13 and 14 because
our</font><a name="_DV_M29" id="_DV_M29"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:10pt;">definitive
proxy statement</font><a name="_DV_C12" id="_DV_C12"></a>
<font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none;">
will not</font><a name="_DV_M31" id="_DV_M31"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:10pt;">be
filed within 120 days</font> <a name="_DV_C14" id=
"_DV_C14"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none;">after</font>
<font style="display: inline;font-size:10pt;">December&nbsp;31,
2017,</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><a name="_DV_C16"
id="_DV_C16"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none;">the
end of the fiscal year covered by our Annual
Report</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:10pt;">on
Form 10-K.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 10.5pt;text-indent:36pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;line-height:100%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-size:10pt;">The Reading Board of
Directors has not yet set a date for the Company’s Annual Meeting
of Stockholders (the “Annual Meeting”).&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 10.5pt;text-indent:36pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;line-height:100%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_C17" id="_DV_C17"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:none;">In
addition, pursuant to the rules of the SEC, we have also included
as exhibits currently dated certifications required under Section
302 of The Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002. Because no financial
statements are contained within this Amendment, we are not
including certifications pursuant to Section 906 of The
Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002. We are amending Part IV to reflect the
inclusion of those certifications.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 10.5pt;text-indent:36pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-decoration:none;line-height:100%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

as described above, no other changes have been made to the Original
Filing. Except as otherwise indicated herein, this Amendment
continues to speak as of the date of the Original Filing, and we
have not updated the disclosures contained therein to reflect any
events that occurred subsequent to the date of the Original Filing.
The filing of this Annual Report on Form 10-K/A is not a
representation that any statements contained in items of our Annual
Report on Form 10-K other than Part III, Items 10 through 14, and
Part IV are true or complete as of any date subsequent to the
Original Filing.</font></p>

<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 18pt;text-indent: -18pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 8pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">﻿</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In addition to the
above referenced standing committees, we have two special
committees.&nbsp;&nbsp;We have a Special Independent Committee,
chaired</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">by</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">our Lead Independent Director,
William Gould, on which Directors Codding and McEachern (the chair
of our Audit Committee) also serve, and a Special Litigation
Committee, also chaired by our Lead Independent Director, William
Gould, on which Director Codding also serves.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Special Independent Committee was formed on</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">August&nbsp;7, 2017, among other
things, to review, consider, deliberate, investigate, analyze,
explore, evaluate, monitor and exercise general oversight of any
and all activities of the Company directly or indirectly involving,
responding to or relating to the purported derivative litigation
brought by Mr.&nbsp;James J. Cotter, Jr. and which remains pending
against certain of our directors (the “</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Cotter, Jr.</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Derivative</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Action”)</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">, the</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">employment arbitration between our
Company and Mr.&nbsp;James J. Cotter, Jr. relating to the
termination of Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr., as our president and chief
executive officer (the “Cotter Jr.</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Employment Arbitration”), the
litigation between Ms.&nbsp;Ellen Cotter and Margaret Cotter (as
Co-Trustees of the James J. Cotter, Sr. Living Trust (the “Cotter
Living Trust”) and Mr.&nbsp;James J. Cotter, Jr. (the “Cotter Trust
Litigation”), and any other litigation or arbitration matters
involving any one or more of Ellen Cotter, Margaret Cotter, James
J. Cotter, Jr., the Estate of James J. Cotter, Sr. (the “Cotter
Estate”) and/or the Cotter Living</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Special
Litigation Committee was formed on April&nbsp;13, 2018, to review
the Cotter, Jr., Derivative Action and to determine whether the
continuance of that litigation is in the best interests of our
Company and thereafter to take such actions as the Special
Litigation Committee may determine to be
appropriate.&nbsp;&nbsp;For more information about the Cotter Jr.
Derivative Action, the Cotter Jr. Employment Arbitration, and the
Cotter Trust Litigation see the disclosure in our Annual Report on
Form 10-K filed on March&nbsp;16, 2018, under the “Part I, Item 1A-
“Risk Factors—Ownership and Management Structure, Corporate
Governance, and Change of Control Risks,” and Part II, Item 8
(Financial Statements and Supplementary Data)--Note 12 –
Commitments and Contingencies to the Consolidated Financial
Statements.”</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In recognition of the
special risks involved with technology and cyber security, Director
Guy Adams has been appointed to serve as our Lead Technology and
Cyber Risk Director.&nbsp;&nbsp;In this role, Director Adams will
be serving as our Board’s liaison with our CEO, CFO and General
Counsel in connection with the assessment of our Company’s
technology and cyber security needs and the implementation of
appropriate policies and procedures to meet those
needs.&nbsp;&nbsp;He will ensure that relevant information is
brought to our Board, and coordinate the timely presentation of
such information to and facilitate the consideration of such
information by all Directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;He will also coordinate
with Management timely and appropriate director education with
respect to such matters so as to enhance director understanding of
the issues involved and the options available to our
Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;In preparation for this role, Director Adams
recently completed the Cyber-Risk Oversight course presented by the
National Association of Corporate Directors.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Board of Directors
held eleven meetings in 2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;All of our Directors
attended at least 75% of such meetings.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M41" id="_DV_M41"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">3</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Ellen M.
Cotter</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">&nbsp;Ellen M. Cotter has been a member of our
Board of Directors since March&nbsp;13, 2013, and currently serves
as a member of our Executive Committee.&nbsp;&nbsp;Ms.&nbsp;Cotter

<font style="display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">James J.

served as the Chief Executive Officer of that company from July
2004 until 2013.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr. served as a

1999 to March 2002. Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr. also</font> <font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">

of a captive insurance company providing insurance for the Cotter
family agricultural activities</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">He was an attorney in the law firm of Winston
&amp; Strawn (and its predecessor), specializing in corporate law,
from September 1997 to May 2004.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr. is
the brother of Margaret Cotter and Ellen M.
Cotter.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr. is a Co-Trustee of the
Cotter Foundation, which is the record holder of 102,751 shares of
Class A Stock and is a Co-Trustee of the Cotter 2005 Grandchildren’
s Trust, which is the record holder of 274,390 shares of Class A
Stock. Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr. has contended that he is a Co-Trustee
with Ellen M. Cotter and Margaret Cotter of the Cotter Living
Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;On March&nbsp;23, 2018, the Superior Court in the
Cotter Trust Litigation ruled in effect, that Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr.,
is not a Co-Trustee of the Cotter Living Trust.</font><a name=
"_DV_M54" id="_DV_M54"></a></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M55" id="_DV_M55"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;Cotter Jr., does not sit on our Board
of Directors based upon the nomination or recommendation of our
Board of Directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;Rather, he was nominated and elected
from the floor at our last Annual Meeting of Stockholders based on
the nomination and vote of Ellen M. Cotter and Margaret Cotter,
acting in their capacities as the Co-Executors of the Cotter Estate
and the Co-Trustees of the Cotter Living Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;As
explained in our Company’s proxy materials for that meeting, before
taking this action, Ellen M. Cotter and Margaret Cotter advised the
Board that, as there remained uncertainty as to whether or not they
were obligated as Trustees of the Cotter Living Trust to continue
Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Jr., on the Board, they would continue to use
their voting power to maintain him as a director.&nbsp;&nbsp;On
March&nbsp;23, 2018, the California Superior Court issued its
determination that the document containing the provision regarding
Mr.&nbsp;Cotter Jr’s continued service as a director of our Company
was invalid.&nbsp;</font> <a name="_DV_M56" id="_DV_M56"></a></p>

accountancy at Claremont McKenna College</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;McEachern was an audit partner
from July&nbsp;1985 to May 2009 with the audit firm of Deloitte
&amp; Touche, LLP, with client concentrations in financial
institutions and real estate</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;McEachern was also a Professional
Accounting Fellow with the Federal Home Loan Bank board in
Washington DC, from June&nbsp;1983 to
July&nbsp;1985</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">From June&nbsp;1976 to June&nbsp;1983,
Mr.&nbsp;McEachern was a staff member and subsequently a manager
with the audit firm of Touche Ross &amp; Co. (predecessor to
Deloitte &amp; Touche, LLP)</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;McEachern received a B.S. in Business
Administration in 1974 from the University of California, Berkeley,
and an M.B.A. in 1976 from the University of Southern
California.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M65" id="_DV_M65"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;McEachern brings to our Board his more
than 40 years’ experience meeting the accounting and auditing needs
of financial institutions and real estate clients, including our
Company</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;McEachern also brings his experience
reporting as an independent auditor to the boards of directors of a
variety of public reporting companies and as a board member himself
for various companies and not-for-profit organizations.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M66" id="_DV_M66"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Michael
Wrotniak</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">.&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">Michael Wrotniak has been a Director of our
Company since October&nbsp;12, 2015, and has served as a member of
our Audit Committee since October&nbsp;25, 2015, and as a member of
our Compensation Committee since November&nbsp;7,
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;Since 2009, Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak has been the Chief
Executive Officer of Aminco Resources, LLC (“Aminco”), a privately
held international commodities trading
firm.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak joined Aminco in 1991 and is
credited with expanding Aminco’s activities in Europe and
Asia.&nbsp;&nbsp;By establishing a joint venture with a Swiss
engineering company, as well as creating partnerships with
Asia-based businesses, Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak successfully diversified
Aminco’s product portfolio.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak became a
partner of Aminco in 2002.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak is a member
of the Board of Advisors of the Little Sisters of the Poor at their
nursing home in the Bronx, New York since approximately
2004.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak graduated from Georgetown
University in 1989 with a B.S. in Business Administration (cum
laude).</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M67" id="_DV_M67"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak is a specialist in foreign
trade, and brings to our Board his considerable experience in
international business, including foreign exchange risk
mitigation.</font></p>

<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Devasis (
“Dev”) Ghose</font><font style="display: inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Dev
Ghose was appointed Chief Financial Officer and Treasurer on
May&nbsp;11, 2015, Executive Vice President on March&nbsp;10, 2016
and served as our Corporate Secretary from April&nbsp;28, 2016
until March&nbsp;9, 2018.&nbsp;&nbsp;Over the past 25 years,
Mr.&nbsp;Ghose has served as Executive Vice President and Chief
Financial Officer and in a number of senior finance roles with
three NYSE-listed companies:&nbsp;&nbsp;Skilled Healthcare Group (a
health services company, now part of Genesis HealthCare) from 2008
to 2013, Shurgard Storage Centers, Inc. (an international company
focused on the acquisition, development and operation of
self-storage centers in the US and Europe; now part of Public
Storage) from 2004 to 2006, and HCP, Inc., (which invests primarily
in real estate serving the healthcare industry) from 1986 to 2003,
and as Managing Director-International for Green Street Advisors
(an independent research and trading firm concentrating on publicly
traded real estate corporate securities in the US &amp; Europe)
from 2006 to 2007.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior thereto, Mr. Ghose worked
for&nbsp;&nbsp;PriceWaterhouseCoopers in the U.S. and KPMG in the
UK from 1975 to 1985.&nbsp;&nbsp;He is a U.S. CPA and a UK
Chartered Accountant, with a B.Sc. in Physics from the University
of Delhi, India and an Executive M.B.A. from UCLA.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M71" id="_DV_M71"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Robert F.
Smerling</font><font style="display: inline;">.&nbsp;</font>
<font style="display: inline;">Robert F. Smerling has served as
President of our domestic cinema operations since
1994.&nbsp;&nbsp;He has been involved in the acquisition and/or
development of all of our existing cinemas.&nbsp;
Prior&nbsp;&nbsp;to joining our Company, Mr.&nbsp;Smerling was the
President of Loews Theaters, at that time a wholly owned subsidiary
of Sony.&nbsp;&nbsp;While at Loews, Mr.&nbsp;Smerling oversaw
operations at some 600 cinemas employing some 6,000 individuals and
the development of more than 25 new multiplex
cinemas.&nbsp;&nbsp;Among Mr.&nbsp;Smerling’s accomplishments at
Loews was the development of the Lincoln Square Cinema Complex with
IMAX in New York City, which continues today to be one of the top
five grossing cinemas in the United States.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to
Mr.&nbsp;Smerling’s employment at Loews, he was Vice Chairman of
USA Cinemas in Boston, and President of Cinemanational
Theatres.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Smerling, a recognized leader in our
industry, has been a director of the National Association of
Theater Owners, the principal trade group representing the cinema
exhibition industry.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M72" id="_DV_M72"></a><a name="_DV_M73" id=
"_DV_M73"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Andrzej J.
Matyczynski</font><font style=
"display: inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski was appointed
as our Executive Vice President—Global Operations on March&nbsp;10,
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;From May&nbsp;11, 2015 until March&nbsp;10, 2016,
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski acted as the Strategic Corporate Advisor to
the Company, and served as our Chief Financial Officer and
Treasurer from November 1999 until May&nbsp;11, 2015 and as
Corporate Secretary from May&nbsp;10, 2011 to October&nbsp;20,
2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to joining our Company, he spent 20 years in
various senior roles throughout the world at Beckman Coulter Inc.,
a U.S. based multi-national
corporation.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski earned a Master’s
Degree in Business Administration from the University of Southern
California.</font></p>

<p style=

<a name="_DV_M75" id="_DV_M75"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Section 16(a) of the Exchange Act requires our
executive officers and Directors, and persons who own more than 10%
of our common stock, to file reports regarding ownership of, and
transactions in, our securities with the Securities and Exchange
Commission (the “SEC”) and to provide us with copies of those
filings.&nbsp;&nbsp;Based solely on our review of the copies
received by us and on the written representations of certain
reporting persons, we believe that the following Form 4’s for
transactions that occurred in 2017 were not filed or filed later
than is required under Section 16(a) of the Securities Exchange Act
of 1934:</font></p>

<a name="_DV_M80" id="_DV_M80"></a><a name="_Toc447217858" id=
"_Toc447217858"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Code of Business Conduct and
Ethics</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M81" id="_DV_M81"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">We have adopted a Code of Business Conduct and
Ethics (the “Code of Conduct”) designed to help our Directors and
employees resolve ethical issues.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Code of Conduct
applies to all Directors and employees, including the Chief
Executive Officer, the Chief Financial Officer, principal
accounting officer, controller and persons performing similar
functions.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Code of Conduct is posted on our website
athttp://www.readingrdi.com/about/#policies-and-guidelines</font><a name="_DV_M82"
id="_DV_M82"></a><font style="display: inline;">.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M83" id="_DV_M83"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The Board has established a means for employees
to report a violation or suspected violation of the Code of Conduct
anonymously.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, we have adopted the “Amended
and Restated Whistleblower Policy and Procedures,” which are posted
on our website, at</font><a name="_DV_M84" id="_DV_M84"></a>
<font style=
"display: inline;">http://www.readingrdi.com/about/#</font><font style="display: inline;">p</font><font style="display: inline;">olicies-and-guidelines,
that establishes a process by which employees may anonymously
disclose to the Audit Committee alleged fraud or violations of
accounting, internal accounting controls or auditing
matters.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M85" id="_DV_M85"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Nomination
Procedures</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M86" id="_DV_M86"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">There have been no material changes to the
procedures by which stockholders may recommend nominees to our
Board of directors, since we last disclosed this
information.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M87" id="_DV_M87"></a><a name="_Hlk512258822" id=
"_Hlk512258822"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">7</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Audit
Committee</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M88" id="_DV_M88"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The Audit Committee operates pursuant to a
Charter adopted by our Board that is available on our website at
http://www.readingrdi.com/about/#committee-charters.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Audit Committee reviews, considers, negotiates and approves or
disapproves related party transactions (see the discussion in the
section entitled “Certain Relationships and Related Party
Transactions” below).&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, the Audit Committee
is responsible for, among other things, (i) reviewing and
discussing with management the Company’s financial statements,
earnings press releases and all internal controls reports, (ii)
appointing, compensating and overseeing the work performed by the
Company’s independent auditors, and (iii) reviewing with the
independent auditors the findings of their audits.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">Our Board has determined that the
Audit Committee is composed entirely of Independent Directors (as
defined in section 5605(a)(2) of the NASDAQ Listing Rules), and
that Mr.&nbsp;Douglas McEachern, the Chair of our Audit Committee,
is qualified as an Audit Committee Financial Expert.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our
Audit Committee is currently composed of Mr.&nbsp;McEachern, who
serves as Chair, Mr.&nbsp;Edward L. Kane and Mr.&nbsp;Michael
Wrotniak.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Audit Committee held nine meetings during
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;All members attended at least 75% of such
meetings.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Compensation and
Stock Options Committee</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">Our Board has established a standing
Compensation Committee consisting of three of our Independent
Directors, and is currently composed of Mr.&nbsp;Edward L. Kane,
who serves as Chair, Dr.&nbsp;Judy Codding and Mr.&nbsp;Michael
Wrotniak.&nbsp;&nbsp;For more information on our Compensatoin
Committee, see&nbsp;&nbsp;Item 11 – Executive
Compensation--Compensation Discussion and Analysis”
below.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensaton&nbsp;&nbsp;Committee held ten
meetings during 2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;All members attended at least 75%
of such meetings.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">﻿</font><a name="_DV_M89" id=
"_DV_M89"></a><a name="_DV_M90" id="_DV_M90"></a></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Item 11</font>
<font style="display: inline;">– &nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Executive
Compensation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M91" id="_DV_M91"></a><a name="_Toc447217877" id=
"_Toc447217877"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Compensation Discussion and
Analysis</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M92" id="_DV_M92"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Role and
Authority of the Compensation Committee</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M93" id="_DV_M93"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Background</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M94" id="_DV_M94"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">As a Controlled Company, we are exempt from the
NASDAQ Listing Rules regarding the determination of executive
compensation solely by independent
directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding such exemption, we have
established a standing Compensation Committee consisting of three
of our Independent Directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee
charter requires our Compensation Committee members to meet the
independence rules and regulations of the Securities Exchange
Commission and the</font> <a name="_DV_C32" id=
"_DV_C32"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">NASDAQ</font><a name="_DV_M95"
id="_DV_M95"></a> <font style="display: inline;">Stock
Market.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Our Executive
Compensation Philosophy</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">Our executive compensation
philosophy is to: (1) attract and retain talented and dedicated
management team members; (2) provide overall compensation as
competitive in our industry; (3) correlate annual cash bonuses to
the achievement of our business and financial objectives; and (4)
provide management team members with appropriate long-term
incentives aligned with stockholder value.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">8</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Our Executive
Compensation Practices At A Glance</font></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style=
"border-collapse:collapse;width: 100.00%;line-height:100%;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:0pt;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"width:50.32%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 2pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-size:2pt;">﻿</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"width:49.68%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000 ;text-align:center;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">What We
Do</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #000000 ;text-align:center;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">What We Do NOT
Do</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">pay for performance&nbsp;&nbsp;Our
Short-Term Incentive Bonuses for our NEO’s are tied to meeting our
Company and individual performance goals</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">NO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">pledging permitted by directors or
Section&nbsp;16 officers without prior notice to Compliance Officer
and Audit Committee Chair</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">provide minimum vesting periods for
our long-term incentive awards</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">NO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">individual hedging or derivative
transactions permitted by directors or Section&nbsp;16
officers</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">empower Board to clawback short term
incentive compensation if there is an accounting restatement due to
material noncompliance with securities laws.</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">NO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">“single trigger” change in control
payments for the benefit of our NEO’s</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">use an independent compensation
consultant</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">NO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">golden parachute tax gross
ups</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">appoint a Compensation Committee
comprised solely of independent directors even though not
required.</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:50.32%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">DO</font>
<font style="display: inline;">require NEO’s and Directors to meet
Company stock ownership requirements</font></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" style=
"border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;width:49.68%;padding:0pt 6.5pt">
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</td>
</tr>

<font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">
1</font> <font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Under our
Compensation Committee Charter, “executive officer” is defined to
mean the chief executive officer, president, chief financial
officer, general counsel, principal accounting officer, any
executive vice president of the Company and any managing director
of Reading Entertainment Australia, Pty Ltd and/or Reading New
Zealand, Ltd.</font></p>

<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">﻿</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">In the first quarter of 2017, our
Compensation Committee, following consultation with its independent
compensation consultant, Willis Towers Watson, our Chief Executive
Officer, and our legal counsel, reviewed the Company’s compensation
levels, programs and practices.&nbsp;&nbsp;Willis Towers Watson
prepared materials that measured our executive and management
compensation against compensation paid by peer group companies
based on the 25th, 50th and 75th percentile of such peer
group.&nbsp;&nbsp;The 50th percentile was the median compensation
paid by such peer group and surveyed companies to executives
performing similar responsibilities and duties.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
summary included base salary, short term incentive (cash bonus) and
long term incentive (equity awards) of the peer and surveyed
companies to the base salary, short term incentive and long term
incentive provided to our executives and
management.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M117" id="_DV_M117"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">For 2017, our Compensation Committee, generally
compared the compensation levels of our NEO’s with the compensation
levels of executives at the following entities which we refer to as
“our peer group:”&nbsp;</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">Acadia Realty Trust, Cedar Realty Trust Inc.,
Charter Hall Retail REIT, Global Eagle Entertainment Inc., IMAX
Corporation, Kite Realty Group Trust, The Marcus
Corporation,</font><font style=
"display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;">National CineMedia, Inc., Pennsylvania Real
Estate Investment Trust, Ramco-Gershenson Properties Trust, Red
Lion Hotels Corporation, Retail Opportunity Investments Corp., Saul
Centers Inc., Urstadt Biddle Properties Inc., and Village Roadshow
Ltd.</font><a name="_DV_M118" id="_DV_M118"></a><a name="_DV_M119"
id="_DV_M119"></a><a name="_DV_M120" id="_DV_M120"></a><a name=
"_DV_M121" id="_DV_M121"></a><a name="_DV_M122" id=
"_DV_M122"></a><a name="_DV_M123" id="_DV_M123"></a><a name=
"_DV_M124" id="_DV_M124"></a><a name="_DV_M125" id=
"_DV_M125"></a><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><a name=
"_DV_M126" id="_DV_M126"></a><a name="_DV_M131" id="_DV_M131"></a>
<font style="display: inline;">Our Compensation Committee
established (i) 2017 annual base salaries at levels that it
believed were generally competitive with executives in our peer
group as described in the executive pay summary assessment prepared
by Willis Towers Watson, except for the base salary of our CEO,
which remains below the 25</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font>
<font style="display: inline;">percentile of our peer group, (ii)
short term incentives in the form of discretionary annual cash
bonuses based on the achievement of identified goals and
benchmarks, and (iii) long-term incentives in the form of employee
stock options and restricted stock units (“RSUs”) that are used as
a retention tool and as a means to further align an executive’s
long-term interests with those of our stockholders, with the
ultimate objective of affording our executives an appropriate
incentive to help drive increases in stockholder value.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M132" id="_DV_M132"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">In the future, it is anticipated that our
Compensation Committee will continue to evaluate both executive
performance and compensation to maintain our ability to attract and
retain highly-qualified executives in key positions and to assure
that compensation provided to executives remains competitive when
compared to the compensation paid to similarly situated executives
of companies with whom we compete for executive talent or that we
consider comparable to our company.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">﻿</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

"display: inline;">______________________________</font></p>

<font style=
"display: inline;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">
2</font> <font style="display: inline;">While this CD&amp;A is
focused on our NEO’s, the same process described for our NEO’s is
followed in setting compensation for all our “Executive Officers.”
</font></p>

"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 72pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">﻿</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M138" id="_DV_M138"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Compensation Committee
performed an annual review of 2017 NEO compensation in the first
quarter of 2018, with a presentation by our Chief Executive Officer
regarding each element of NEO compensation
arrangements.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee reviewed the
performance goals of our NEO’s and the extent to which the NEO
achieved such goals.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee, in
determining final incentive compensation for services rendered in
2017, also considered, among other things, the recommendations of
our Chief Executive Officer, the overall operating results of our
Company and the challenges met in achieving those operating
results.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">As part of the NEO
compensation review, our Chief Executive Officer recommended, in
certain cases, other changes to an NEO’s compensation arrangements
such as to effect a change in the executive’s
responsibilities.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee evaluated
the Chief Executive Officer’s recommendations and, in its
discretion, accepted or rejected the recommendations, subject to
the terms of any written employment agreements.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M139" id="_DV_M139"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">In the first quarter of 2018, our
Compensation Committee met separately and with our Chief Executive
Officer to review the performance goals of our various officers and
to determine the extent to which the officer achieved such
goals.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee, in determining final
incentive compensation for services rendered in 2017, also
considered, among other things, the recommendations of our Chief
Executive Officer, the overall operating results of our Company and
the challenges met in achieving those operating results.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">The Compensation
Committee noted the following with respect to 2017:</font></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0"
cellspacing="0">
<tr>
<td style="width:36pt;">
<p style="width:36pt;font-size:0pt;"></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
<p style=

"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M140" id="_DV_M140"></a><a name="_DV_M141" id=

"_DV_M168"></a><a name="_DV_M169" id="_DV_M169"></a><a name=
"_DV_M170" id="_DV_M170"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">CEO
Compensation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M171" id="_DV_M171"></a><a name="_DV_M172" id=
"_DV_M172"></a><a name="_DV_M173" id="_DV_M173"></a><a name=
"_DV_M174" id="_DV_M174"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">For 2017, our Compensation
Committee met in executive sessions without our Chief Executive
Officer to consider the Chief Executive Officer’s compensation,
including base salary, cash bonus and equity award, if
any.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to such executive sessions, our Compensation
Committee interviewed our Chief Executive Officer to obtain a
better understanding of factors contributing to the Chief Executive
Officer's compensation.&nbsp;&nbsp;With the exception of these
executive sessions of our Compensation Committee, as a rule, our
Chief Executive Officer participated in all deliberations of the
Compensation Committee relating to NEO
compensation.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, our Compensation Committee also
asked our Chief Executive Officer to be excused for certain
deliberations with respect to the compensation recommended for
Margaret Cotter, the sister of our Chief Executive
Officer.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M175" id="_DV_M175"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">The Base Salary set for our Chief
Executive Officer for 2017, or $463,800, remains substantially
below the market base salary median for our peer
group.&nbsp;&nbsp;By comparison, the Willis Towers Watson report
showed that the 25</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">,
50</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">and
75</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">percentiles in the
peer group of CEO base salaries were $529,000, $627,000 and
$717,000, respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;Because Ms.&nbsp;Cotter’s
potential short term incentive payment was based on a percentage
(95%) of her base salary,</font> <a name="_DV_C90" id=
"_DV_C90"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">which
was below the 25</font><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font>
<font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">
percentile of market peers</font><a name="_DV_M176" id=
"_DV_M176"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">,
&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Ms.&nbsp;Cotter</font><a name=
"_DV_M177" id="_DV_M177"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">’s potential short term incentive
payment</font><a name="_DV_C93" id="_DV_C93"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">was
also set to be in a lower range than market peers.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M178" id="_DV_M178"></a><a name="_DV_M179" id=
"_DV_M179"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">2017
Base Salaries</font></p>
<p style=

<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M185" id="_DV_M185"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">2017
Short Term Incentives</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp; &nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M186" id="_DV_M186"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">The Short Term Incentives
authorized by our Compensation Committee provide our NEOs with an
opportunity to earn an annual cash bonus based upon the achievement
of certain of our Company’s financial goals, division goals and
individual goals, established by our Chief Executive Officer and
approved by our Compensation Committee during the first quarter of
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;Under our Compensation Committee
Charter,&nbsp;&nbsp;the compensation payable to our Chief Executive
Officer, Ellen Cotter, and Margaret Cotter must also be approved by
our Board. Participants</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">in
the short-term incentive plan are advised of his or her annual
potential target bonus expressed as a percentage of the participant’
s base salary and by dollar amount.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">For 2017, the
performance goals for our NEOs included (i) a target for a
Company-wide Performance Goal Operational Metric based upon
Company-wide “Compensation Adjusted EBITDA”</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">(a
non-GAAP measure defined below); and (ii) Company-wide Performance
Goal Development Metrics, (iii) Division Performance Goal
Operational Metrics</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">3</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">,
and (iv) Division Performance Goal Development
Metrics.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, each of our NEOs was provided
individually tailored goals based on the NEO’s respective areas of
responsibility, which goals were approved by our Compensation
Committee.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">﻿</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">______________________________</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:6pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">
3</font> <font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Chief
Executive Officer and Chief</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Financial</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Officer did not have “divisional”
based goal metrics.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
</p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">Management and the Compensation
Committee use “Earnings before Interest, Taxes, Depreciation and
Amortization, or “EBITDA,” a non-GAAP financial measure, for a
number of purposes in assessing the performance of the Company. See
Item 6 – Selected Financial Data for a discussion and
reconciliation of EBITDA.&nbsp;&nbsp;“Compensation Adjusted EBITDA”
is one of the two principal Company-wide performance metrics used
by the Compensation Committee and for assessing the performance of
executives of the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;Compensation Adjusted EBITDA
is not otherwise used by management and is calculated in a manner
intended to adjust out of EBITDA those elements not generally
within the control of our executives, considering the precision of
the annual operating and capital expenditure budgets and the
circumstances during the year.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">In the first quarter of 2017, our
Compensation Committee set the following Company-wide Adjusted
EBITDA targets:</font></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0"
cellspacing="0">
<tr>
<td style="width:36pt;">
<p style="width:36pt;font-size:0pt;"></p>
</td>
<td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
<p style=
"text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;">
<font style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;;">
(i)</font></p>
</td>
<td style="width:0pt;">
<p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top">
<p style=
"text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Threshold –
$40,050,000</font></p>

<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Ellen M. Cotter</font>
<font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">
is</font> <font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">our
President and Chief Executive Officer</font><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Her</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">target bonus
opportunity was 95% of Base Salary.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the
Company-wide goals, our Compensation Committee concluded that 90%
of her Annual Performance Goals had been met.&nbsp;&nbsp;Her
individual Annual Performance Goals included developing a
stronger</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">human
resources function; achieving substantial progress on future value
creation opportunities; achieving certain goals for the Cinemas
1,2,3 Project; achieving certain investor relations objectives,
succession planning and construction management
enhancements.&nbsp;&nbsp;Further, our Compensation Committee
considered other subjective factors including her roles on behalf
of the Company with respect to the Cotter, Jr. Derivative
Litigation, and the Courtenay Central, NZ
Earthquake.&nbsp;&nbsp;Based on our Compensation Committee’s
review, Ms.&nbsp;Cotter was awarded a bonus of $374,474, which was
also approved by our Board.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Robert Smerling is
President of US Cinemas.&nbsp;&nbsp;His target bonus opportunity
was 30% of Base Salary</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In addition to the
Company-wide goals, our Compensation Committee concluded that
certain of his Division Goals and certain of his Annual Performance
Goals had been met.&nbsp;&nbsp;His divisional
and&nbsp;&nbsp;individual goals related to achieving certain
milestones in our US cinema circuit (i) capex program, (ii)
operational strategies and (iii) lease negotiations with respect to
certain cinema locations. Based on our Compensation Committee’s
review, Mr.&nbsp;Smerling was awarded a bonus
of&nbsp;&nbsp;$70,439.</font></p>

<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M285" id="_DV_M285"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Compensation Committee has
generally discussed, but has not yet seriously evaluated, future
consideration of adding a performance condition to the long-term
incentive awards.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M286" id="_DV_M286"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">Other
Elements of Compensation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M287" id="_DV_M287"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">Retirement
Plans</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M288" id="_DV_M288"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">We maintain a 401(k) retirement
savings plan that allows eligible employees to defer a portion of
their compensation, within limits prescribed by the Internal
Revenue Code, on a pre-tax basis through contributions to the
plan.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our NEOs are eligible to participate in the 401(k)
plan on the same terms as other full-time employees
generally.&nbsp;&nbsp;Currently, we match contributions made by
participants in the 401(k) plan up to a specified percentage, and
these matching contributions are fully vested as of the date on
which the contribution is made.&nbsp;&nbsp;We believe that
providing a vehicle for tax-deferred retirement savings through our
401(k) plan, and making fully vested matching contributions, adds
to the overall desirability of our executive compensation package
and further incentivizes our employees, including our NEOs, in
accordance with our compensation policies.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M289" id="_DV_M289"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">14</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">Other Retirement
Plans</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M290" id="_DV_M290"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">During 2012, Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski was granted an
unfunded, nonqualified deferred compensation plan (“DCP”) that was
partially vested and was to vest further so long as he remained in
our continuous employ.&nbsp;&nbsp;The DCP allowed
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski to defer part of the cash portion of his
compensation, subject to annual limits set forth in the
DCP.&nbsp;&nbsp;The funds held pursuant to the DCP are not
segregated and do not accrue interest or other
earnings.&nbsp;&nbsp;If Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski were to be terminated
for cause, then the total vested amount would be reduced to
zero.&nbsp;&nbsp;The incremental amount vested each year was made
subject to review and approval by our Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;Please see
the “</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">Nonqualified Deferred
Compensation</font><font style="display: inline;">” table for
additional information.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition,
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski is entitled to a lump-sum severance payment of
$50,000, provided there has been no termination for cause and
subject to certain offsets, upon his retirement.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M291" id="_DV_M291"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Upon the termination of Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski’s
employment, he will also be entitled under the DCP agreement to
payment of the vested benefits under his DCP in annual installments
following the later of (a) 30 days following Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski’s
65th birthday or (b) six months after his separation from service
for reasons other than his death or termination for
cause.&nbsp;&nbsp;The DCP was to vest over 7 years and with full
vesting to occur in 2019 at $1,000,000 in deferred
compensation.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, in connection with his changed
employment to EVP - Global Operations, the Company and
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski agreed that the Company would cease making
contributions to the DCP on April&nbsp;15, 2016 and that the final
contributions by the Company to the DCP would be $150,000 for 2015,
and $21,875 for 2016, satisfying the Company’s total contribution
obligations under the DCP at an amount of $621,875.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M292" id="_DV_M292"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The DCP is an unfunded contractual obligation of
the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;DCP benefits are paid from the general
assets of the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, the Company reserves the
right to establish a grantor trust from which DCP benefits may be
paid.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M293" id="_DV_M293"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">In March 2016, the Compensation Committee
approved a one-time retirement benefit for Robert Smerling,
President, US Cinemas, due to his significant long term service to
the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;The retirement benefit is</font> <a name=
"_DV_C204" id="_DV_C204"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">a
single year benefit in</font><a name="_DV_M294" id="_DV_M294"></a>
<font style="display: inline;">an amount equal to the average of
the two highest total cash compensation (base salary plus cash
bonus) years paid to Mr.&nbsp;Smerling in the then most recently
completed five year period.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M295" id="_DV_M295"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">We currently maintain no other retirement plan
for our NEOs.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M296" id="_DV_M296"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">Key Person
Insurance</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M297" id="_DV_M297"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">We maintain life insurance on certain
individuals who we believe to be key to our management, including
certain NEOs.&nbsp;&nbsp;If such individual ceases to be our
employee or independent contractor, as the case may be, she or he
is permitted, by assuming responsibility for all future premium
payments, to replace our Company as the beneficiary under such
policy.&nbsp;&nbsp;These policies allow each such individual to
purchase up to an equal amount of insurance for such individual’s
own benefit.&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of our employees, the premium
for both the insurance as to which we are the beneficiary and the
insurance as to which our employee is the beneficiary, is paid by
us.&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of NEOs, the premium paid by us for the
benefit of such individual is reflected in the Compensation Table
in the column captioned “All Other Compensation.”</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M298" id="_DV_M298"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">Employee Benefits and
Perquisites</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M299" id="_DV_M299"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Our NEOs are eligible to participate in our
health and welfare plans to the same extent as all full-time
employees generally.&nbsp;&nbsp;We do not generally provide our
NEOs with perquisites or other personal
benefits.&nbsp;&nbsp;Historically,</font> <a name="_DV_C206" id=
"_DV_C206"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">certain</font><a name="_DV_M300"
id="_DV_M300"></a> <font style="display: inline;">of our other NEOs
also received an automobile allowance.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Tax and
Accounting Considerations</font><font style=
"display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M305" id="_DV_M305"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">Deductibility of Executive
Compensation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M306" id="_DV_M306"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Subject to an exception for “performance-based
compensation,” Section 162(m) of the Internal Revenue Code
generally prohibits publicly held corporations from deducting for
federal income tax purposes annual compensation paid to any senior
executive officer to the extent that such annual compensation
exceeds $1.0&nbsp;million.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Compensation Committee
and our Board consider the limits on deductibility under Section
162(m) in establishing executive compensation, but retain the
discretion to authorize the payment of compensation that exceeds
the limit on deductibility under this Section.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M307" id="_DV_M307"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;">Nonqualified Deferred
Compensation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M308" id="_DV_M308"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">We believe we are operating, where applicable,
in compliance with the tax rules applicable to nonqualified
deferred compensation arrangements.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M309" id="_DV_M309"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">15</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Say on
Pay</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M310" id="_DV_M310"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">At our Annual Meeting of Stockholders held on
November&nbsp;7, 2017, we held an advisory vote on executive
compensation.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our stockholders voted in favor of our
Company’s executive compensation, as well as in favor to change the
“say on pay” vote to an annual vote.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Compensation
Committee reviewed the results of the advisory vote on executive
compensation in 2017 and did not make any changes to our
compensation based on the results of the vote.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our next
advisory vote of our stockholders on executive compensation will be
at our 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Policy on Stock
Ownership</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Courier New;line-height:100%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-family:Times New Roman;">At its
meeting held on March&nbsp;23, 2017, our Board determined that, as
a matter of policy, directors should hold shares of the Company’s
common stock having a fair market value equal to not less than
three times (3X) their annual cash retainer, that the chief
executive officer should hold shares of the Company’s common stock
having a fair market value equal to not less than six times (6X)
her base salary, and that all other executive officers (as defined
in the Compensation Committee Charter) should hold shares of the
Company’s common stock having a fair market value equal to not less
than one times (1X) their respective base salaries.&nbsp;&nbsp;In
each case, fair market value would be determined by reference to
the trading price of such securities on the NASDAQ, as measured at
the end of each calendar year.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board further
determined that for purposes of determining requisite stock
ownership, there should be included all shares owned of record or
beneficially, all vested and unvested stock options and all vested
and unvested restricted stock units held by such individual and
that the individuals covered by the policy should have a period of
five years in which to achieve such levels of ownership.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M313" id="_DV_M313"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Executive
Compensation</font></p>

"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In addition to the
compensation set forth herein for our NEO’s, we
are&nbsp;&nbsp;providing the following compensation information for
our General Counsel, S. Craig Tompkins.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. Tompkins was
employed by the Company on June&nbsp;1, 2017, as our Company’s
non-executive General Counsel.&nbsp;&nbsp;From June&nbsp;1, 2017
through December&nbsp;31, 2017, the salary received by Mr. Tompkins
as an employee was $248,000.&nbsp;&nbsp;This amount does not
include cash compensation paid to Mr. Tompkins prior to
June&nbsp;1, 2017 when Mr. Tompkins was an independent
contractor.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In 2017, Mr. Tompkins
was granted 5-year options to acquire 37,262 shares of Class A
Common Stock at exercise prices of $15.97 and $15.67 and RSUs for
11,151 shares of Class A Common Stock.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Following his
employment as General Counsel in 2017, and in connection with his
employment, Mr. Tompkins was granted a separation benefit in an
amount equal to the difference between (a) the average of the two
highest total cash compensation (base salary plus cash bonus) years
paid to Mr. Tomkins in the then most recently completed five year
period and (b) all amounts paid to Mr. Tompkins</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">under</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">a pension plan (the “Craig
Corporation Plan”) established for his benefit when he was an
employee of Craig Corporation (a corporate predecessor of our
Company and now a wholly owned subsidiary of our
Company).&nbsp;&nbsp;The amount paid to Mr. Tompkins in 2017 under
the Craig Corporation Plan was $197,060.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">In 2017, Mr. Tompkins
also received benefits (including 401(k) and key man life
insurance) commensurate with other senior executives of</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">the</font>
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Company.</font></p>

<div style="width:100%">
<p style=

<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
