<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">2010 Equity
Incentive Plan</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M342" id="_DV_M342"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">On May&nbsp;13, 2010, our stockholders approved
the 2010 Stock Incentive Plan at the annual meeting of stockholders
in accordance with the recommendation of our Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Plan provides for awards of stock options, restricted stock, bonus
stock, and stock appreciation rights to eligible employees,
Directors, and consultants.&nbsp;&nbsp;On March&nbsp;10, 2016, our
Board approved a First Amendment to the Plan to permit the award of
restricted stock units. On March&nbsp;2, 2017 and on April&nbsp;26,
2017, our Board approved a further amendment to the Plan (the
Second Amendment to the Plan) (i) to allow net exercises of stock
options to be made at the Participant’s election; (ii) to
incorporate the substance of the resolutions of the Compensation
Committee on May&nbsp;16, 2013 authorizing certain cashless
transactions and automatic exercise of expiring in the money
options; (iii) to broaden the permissible tax withholding by
surrender of shares and (iv) to change the definition of Fair
Market Value for purposes of the calculation of share value for
purposes of net exercises and cashless exercises from the closing
price to the average of the price of the highest sale price and the
lowest sale price on the applicable measured day. On
November&nbsp;7, 2017, our stockholders approved an amendment to
increase the number of shares issuable under the Plan by 947,460
shares.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Plan, as amended, permits issuance of a
maximum of 2,197,460 shares of which, 932,300 has been used to
date.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Plan expires automatically on March&nbsp;11,
2020.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M343" id="_DV_M343"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Equity awards under our Plan are intended by us
to attract and retain qualified management, directors and
consultants, to bind the interests of eligible recipients more
closely to our own interests by offering them opportunities to
acquire our common stock and/or cash and to afford eligible
recipients&nbsp;&nbsp;stock-based compensation opportunities that
are competitive with those afforded by similar
businesses.&nbsp;&nbsp;Equity awards may include stock options,
restricted stock,</font> <a name="_DV_C211" id=
"_DV_C211"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">restricted
stock units,</font> <a name="_DV_M344" id=
"_DV_M344"></a><font style="display: inline;">bonus stock, or stock
appreciation rights.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M345" id="_DV_M345"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">If awarded, it is generally our policy to value
stock options and restricted stock at the average of the high and
low sales price of our common stock as reported on the NASDAQ Stock
Market on the date the award is approved or on the date of hire, if
the stock is granted as a recruitment incentive.&nbsp;&nbsp;When
stock is granted as bonus compensation for a particular
transaction, the award may be based on the market price on a date
calculated from the closing date of the relevant
transaction.&nbsp;&nbsp;Awards may also be subject to vesting and
limitations on voting or other rights.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

</td>

<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M354" id="_DV_M354"></a><a name="_Toc447217889" id=
"_Toc447217889"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Potential
Payments upon Termination of Employment or Change in
Control</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M355" id="_DV_M355"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">The following paragraphs provide
information regarding potential payments to each of our NEOs in
connection with certain termination events, including a termination
related to a change of control of the Company, as of
December&nbsp;31, 2017:</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M356" id="_DV_M356"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">Mr.&nbsp;Dev
Ghose – Separation Payment Benefit</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">.
&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;color:#454545;">Mr.
Ghose's employment contract with our Company expires on
May&nbsp;10, 2018.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;It is currently anticipated
that Mr. Ghose will continue with our Company as an employee under
terms currently being negotiated.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. Ghose will have
upon the expiration of his existing employment contract, a vested
right to receive a payment of twelve months salary and benefits
(determined as of May&nbsp;10, 2018) upon termination or
non-renewal of his employment agreement.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M357" id="_DV_M357"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">Mr.&nbsp;Andrzej
J. Matyczynski – Deferred Compensation Benefits</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;During 2012,
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski was granted an unfunded, nonqualified</font>
<a name="_DV_C213" id="_DV_C213"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">DCP</font><a name="_DV_M358"
id="_DV_M358"></a> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">that was partially vested and was
to vest further so long as he remained in our</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#454545;">continuous</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">employ.&nbsp;&nbsp;If
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski were to be terminated for cause, then the
total vested amount would be reduced to zero.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
incremental amount vested each year was made subject to review and
approval by our Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;Please see the 
“</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">Nonqualified
Deferred Compensation</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">” table for additional
information.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M359" id="_DV_M359"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Upon the termination of
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski’s employment, he will be entitled under the
DCP agreement to payment of the vested benefits under his DCP in
annual installments following the later of (a) 30 days following
Mr.&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#454545;">Matyczynski’s</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">65th birthday or (b) six months
after his separation from service for reasons other than his death
or termination for cause.&nbsp;&nbsp;The DCP was to vest over 7
years and with full vesting to occur in 2019 at $1,000,000 in
deferred compensation.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, in connection with his
employment as EVP Global Operations, the Company and
Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski agreed that the Company would cease making
contributions to the DCP on April&nbsp;15, 2016 and that the final
contributions by the Company to the DCP would be $150,000 for 2015
and $21,875 for 2016, satisfying the Company’s obligations under
the DCP.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski’s agreement contains
nonsolicitation provisions that extend for one year after his
retirement.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M360" id="_DV_M360"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">20</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">Under Mr.&nbsp;Matyczynski’s
agreement, on his retirement date and provided there has not been a
termination for cause, Mr.&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#454545;">Matyczynski</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">will be entitled to a lump sum severance payment
in an amount equal to $50,000, less certain offsets.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M361" id="_DV_M361"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Robert F. Smerling –
Retirement Benefit</font><font style=
"display: inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;In March 2016, the Compensation
Committee approved a one-time retirement benefit for Robert
Smerling, President, Cinema Operations, due to his significant
long-term service to the Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;The retirement benefit
is</font><a name="_DV_C214" id="_DV_C214"></a> <font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">
&nbsp;a</font><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;border-bottom-style:double;border-bottom-width:2pt;color:#000000;height:100%;text-indent:0pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">single
year payment based on</font><a name="_DV_M362" id="_DV_M362"></a>
<font style="display: inline;">the average of the two
highest</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#454545;">total</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">cash compensation (base salary plus cash bonus)
years paid to Mr.&nbsp;Smerling in the then most recently completed
five year period.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

upon</font> <a name="_DV_C221" id="_DV_C221"></a><font style=

recipient’s de</font><a name="_DV_C223" id=

(ii</font><a name="_DV_M370" id="_DV_M370"></a><font style=

"_DV_M372" id="_DV_M372"></a><font style="display: inline;">certain
corporate</font> <a name="_DV_C227" id="_DV_C227"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">transactions in</font> <font style=

which</font><a name="_DV_M374" id="_DV_M374"></a><font style=

"display: inline;">the awards are</font> <a name="_DV_C228" id=
"_DV_C228"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">not</font>
<a name="_DV_M375" id="_DV_M375"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">replaced</font><a name="_DV_M376" id=
"_DV_M376"></a> <font style="display: inline;">with</font> <a name=

<a name="_DV_M379" id="_DV_M379"></a><font style=

“</font><a name="_DV_M380" id="_DV_M380"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">good reason” within twenty-four months of</font>
<a name="_DV_C236" id="_DV_C236"></a><font style=

<a name="_DV_M386" id="_DV_M386"></a><a name="_DV_M387" id=
"_DV_M387"></a><a name="_DV_M388" id="_DV_M388"></a><a name=
"_DV_M389" id="_DV_M389"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Employment
Agreements</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M390" id="_DV_M390"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">As of December&nbsp;31, 2017, our
NEOs had the following employment agreements in
place.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M391" id="_DV_M391"></a><font style=
"display: inline;text-decoration:underline;color:#000000;">Dev
Ghose</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">. On April
20, 2015, we entered into an employment agreement with Mr. Dev
Ghose, pursuant to which he agreed to serve as our Chief Financial
Officer for&nbsp;&nbsp;one-year terms, renewable annually,
commencing on May 11, 2015.&nbsp;&nbsp;The employment agreement
provides that Mr. Ghose is to receive an annual base salary of
$412,000, with an annual target bonus of $206,000, and employee
benefits in line with those received by our other senior
executives.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. Ghose was also granted stock options to
purchase 100,000 shares of Class A Stock at an exercise price equal
to the closing price of our Class A Stock on the date of grant and
which will vest in equal annual increments over a four-year period,
subject to his remaining in our continuous employ through each
annual vesting date.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M392" id="_DV_M392"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Under his employment agreement, we
may terminate Mr.&nbsp;Ghose’s employment with or without cause (as
defined) at any time.&nbsp;&nbsp;If we terminate his employment
without cause or fail to renew his employment agreement upon
expiration without cause, Mr.&nbsp;Ghose will be entitled to
receive severance in an amount equal to the salary and benefits he
was receiving for a period of 12 months following such termination
or non-renewal. If the termination is in connection with a “change
of control” (as defined), Mr.&nbsp;Ghose would be entitled to
severance in an amount equal to the compensation he would have
received for a period two years from such termination.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Mr. Ghose's employment
contract with our Company expires on May&nbsp;10,
2018.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is currently anticipated that Mr. Ghose will
continue with our Company as an employee under terms currently
being negotiated.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. Ghose will have upon the
expiration of his existing employment contract, a vested right to
receive a payment of twelve months salary and benefits (determined
as of May&nbsp;10, 2018) upon termination or non-renewal of is
employment agreement.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

<font style="display: inline;text-decoration:underline;">Andrzej J.

"_Toc447217879" id="_Toc447217879"></a><a name="_Toc447217878" id=
"_Toc447217878"></a><a name="_Toc446123022" id=
"_Toc446123022"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Compensation
Committee Interlocks and Insider Participation</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M401" id="_DV_M401"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Compensation Committee is
currently composed of Mr.&nbsp;Kane, who serves as Chair,
Dr.&nbsp;Codding and</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Mr.&nbsp;Wrotniak.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;McEachern
served on our Compensation Committee until November
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;None of the members of the Compensation Committee
was an officer or employee of the Company at any time during
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;None of our executive officers serves as a member
of the board of directors or compensation committee of any entity
that has or had one or more executive officers serving as a member
of our Board of Directors or Compensation Committee.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">22</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Chief Executive Pay
Ratio</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;text-indent:22.5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">As of
December&nbsp;31, 2017, we employed approximately 2,500 persons,
with more than 85% of such persons being seasonal, part-time
employees.&nbsp; Generally, we have experienced comparatively
higher turnover rates with our seasonal, part</font><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">‑time employees, as compared to
our full-time employees.&nbsp; Accordingly, the median total
compensation we estimate below, as well as the resulting ratio of
Ms.&nbsp;Ellen Cotter’s compensation to such estimated median total
compensation is reflective of both the seasonal, part-time nature
of the majority of our employees, as well as the fact that we
experience a high turnover rate with such employees each fiscal
year.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;text-indent:22.5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">Ms. Ellen Cotter’s,
our President and Chief Executive Officer, for the fiscal year 2017
received total compensation of $1,210,334.&nbsp;&nbsp;We estimate
that the median W-2 (or equivalent) for all Company employees,
excluding our Chief Executive Officer, was $7,465 as of
December&nbsp;31, 2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;As a result, Ms. Ellen Cotter’s
fiscal 2017 total compensation was approximately 162 times greater
than that of the median total compensation for all of our
employees.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;text-indent:22.5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">We identified the
median employee by examining the 2017 W-2 (or equivalent) for all
individuals, excluding our Chief Executive Officer, who were
employed by us on December&nbsp;31, 2017, the last day of our
payroll year (whether employed on a full-time, part-time, or
seasonal basis).&nbsp;&nbsp;For such employees, we did not make any
assumptions, adjustments, or estimates with respect to total
compensation, and we did not annualize the compensation for any
employees that were not employed by us for all of
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;For employees based and paid overseas, we
converted their earnings to US dollars using the average exchange
rates between local currency and US dollars.&nbsp;&nbsp;After
identifying the median employee, we calculated the above total
compensation for such employee using the same methodology we use
for our NEO’s as set forth in the Summary Compensation
Table.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M402" id="_DV_M402"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;text-transform:uppercase;">REPORT
OF THE COMPENSATION COMMITTEE</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M403" id="_DV_M403"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The Compensation Committee has reviewed and
discussed with management the “Compensation Discussion and Analysis”
 required by Item 401(b) of Regulation S-K and, based on such
review and discussions, has recommended to our Board that the
foregoing “Compensation Discussion and Analysis” be included in
this Form 10-K/A.</font></p>

Class A Stock shown includes 21,297 shares subject to stock options
as well as 811,813 shares held directly.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Class A
Stock shown also includes 274,390 shares held by the Cotter 2005
Grandchildren’s Trust and 29,730 shares from the Cotter Profit
Sharing Plan.&nbsp;&nbsp;Margaret Cotter is Co-Trustee of the
Cotter 2005 Grandchildren’s Trust and, as such, is deemed to
beneficially own such shares.&nbsp;&nbsp;Ms. Cotter disclaims
beneficial ownership of such shares except to the extent of her
pecuniary interest, if any, in such shares.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Class A
Stock shown includes 326,800 shares of Class A Stock that are part
of the Cotter Estate.&nbsp;&nbsp;As Co-Executor of the Cotter
Estate, Ms. Cotter would be deemed to beneficially own such
shares.&nbsp;&nbsp;The shares of Class A Stock shown also include
1,897,649 shares held by the Cotter Living Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;See
footnote (12) for information regarding beneficial ownership of the
shares held by the Living Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;As Co-Trustees of the
Living Trust, Ellen Cotter and Margaret Cotter would be deemed to
beneficially own such shares depending upon the outcome of the
matters described in footnote (14).&nbsp;&nbsp;Together Margaret
Cotter and Ellen M. Cotter beneficially own 1,208,988 shares of
Class B Stock.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Class A Stock showng also inmcludeds
102,751 shares held by the Cotter Foundation, of which Ellen
Cotter, Margaret Cotter and James J. Cotter, Jr., are
Co-Trustees.</font></p>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<p style=
"margin:12pt 0pt 10pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 11pt">
<a name="_DV_M417" id="_DV_M417"></a><a name="_DV_M418" id=
"_DV_M418"></a><a name="_DV_M419" id="_DV_M419"></a><a name=
"_DV_M420" id="_DV_M420"></a><a name="_DV_M421" id=
"_DV_M421"></a><a name="_DV_M422" id="_DV_M422"></a><a name=
"_DV_M423" id="_DV_M423"></a><a name="_DV_M424" id=
"_DV_M424"></a><a name="_DV_M425" id="_DV_M425"></a><a name=
"_DV_M426" id="_DV_M426"></a><a name="_DV_M427" id=
"_DV_M427"></a><a name="_DV_M428" id="_DV_M428"></a><a name=
"_DV_M429" id="_DV_M429"></a><a name="_DV_M430" id=
"_DV_M430"></a><a name="_DV_M431" id="_DV_M431"></a><a name=
"_DV_M432" id="_DV_M432"></a><a name="_DV_M433" id=
"_DV_M433"></a><a name="_DV_M434" id="_DV_M434"></a><a name=
"_DV_M435" id="_DV_M435"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;">Item 13</font>
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">–
&nbsp;</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;">Certain
Relationships and Related Transactions, and Director
Independence</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M436" id="_DV_M436"></a><a name="_Toc447217890" id=
"_Toc447217890"></a><a name="_Toc446123023" id=
"_Toc446123023"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;text-transform:uppercase;">CERTAIN
RELATIONSHIPS AND RELATED PARTY TRANSACTIONS</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M437" id="_DV_M437"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The members of our Audit Committee are Douglas
McEachern, who serves as Chair, Edward Kane and Michael
Wrotniak.&nbsp;&nbsp;Management presents all potential related
party transactions to the Audit Committee for
review.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Audit Committee reviews whether a given
related party transaction is beneficial to our Company, and
approves or bars the transaction after a thorough
analysis.&nbsp;&nbsp;Only Committee members disinterested in the
transaction in question participate in the determination of whether
the transaction may proceed.&nbsp;&nbsp;See the discussion entitled
“</font><font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">Review,
Approval or Ratification of Transactions with Related
Persons</font><font style="display: inline;">” for additional
information regarding the review process.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M438" id="_DV_M438"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Sutton Hill Capital</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M439" id="_DV_M439"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">In 2001, we entered into a transaction with
Sutton Hill Capital, LLC (“SHC”) regarding the master leasing, with
an option to purchase, of certain cinemas located in Manhattan
including our Village East and Cinemas 1, 2, 3
theaters.&nbsp;&nbsp;In connection with that transaction, we also
agreed (i) to lend certain amounts to SHC, to provide liquidity in
its investment, pending our determination whether or not to
exercise our option to purchase and (ii) to manage the 86th Street
Cinema on a fee basis.&nbsp;&nbsp;SHC is a limited liability
company owned in equal shares by the Cotter Estate or the Cotter
Living Trust and a third party.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M440" id="_DV_M440"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">As previously reported, over the years, two of
the cinemas subject to the master leasing agreement have been
redeveloped and one (the Cinemas 1, 2, 3 discussed below) has been
acquired.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Village East is the only cinema that
remains subject to this master lease.&nbsp;&nbsp;We paid an annual
rent of $590,000 for this cinema to SHC in each of 2017, 2016 and
2015.&nbsp;&nbsp;During this same period, we received management
fees from the 86</font><font style=
"display: inline;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font>
<font style="display: inline;">Street Cinema of $141,000, $150,000
and $151,000, respectively.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M441" id="_DV_M441"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">In 2005, we acquired (i) from a third party the
fee interest underlying the Cinemas 1, 2, 3&nbsp;&nbsp;and (ii)
from SHC its interest in the ground lease estate underlying and the
improvements constituting the Cinemas 1, 2, 3.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
ground lease estate and the improvements acquired from SHC were
originally a part of the master lease transaction, discussed
above.&nbsp;&nbsp;In connection with that transaction, we granted
to SHC an option to acquire at cost a 25% interest in the special
purpose entity (Sutton Hill Properties, LLC (“SHP”) formed to
acquire these fee, leasehold and improvements
interests.&nbsp;&nbsp;On June&nbsp;28, 2007, SHC exercised this
option, paying $3.0&nbsp;million and assuming a proportionate share
of SHP’s liabilities.&nbsp;&nbsp;At the time of the option exercise
and the closing of the acquisition of the 25% interest, SHP had
debt of $26.9&nbsp;million, including a $2.9&nbsp;million,
non-interest bearing intercompany loan from the
Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;As of December&nbsp;31, 2015, SHP had debt of
$19.4&nbsp;million (again, including the intercompany
loan).&nbsp;&nbsp;Since the acquisition by SHC of its 25% interest,
SHP has covered its operating costs and debt service through cash
flow from the Cinemas 1, 2, 3, (ii) borrowings from third parties,
and (iii) pro-rata contributions from the members.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M442" id="_DV_M442"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">On June&nbsp;29, 2010, we agreed to extend our
existing lease from SHC of the Village East Cinema by 10 years,
with a new termination date of June&nbsp;30, 2020.&nbsp;&nbsp;This
amendment was reviewed and approved by our Audit
Committee.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Village East lease</font> <font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">includes</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">a sub-lease of the ground underlying the cinema
that is subject to a longer-term ground lease between SHC and an
unrelated third party that expires in June&nbsp;2031 (the “cinema
ground lease”).&nbsp;&nbsp;The extended lease provides for a call
option pursuant to which Reading may purchase the cinema ground
lease for $5.9&nbsp;million at the end of the lease
term.&nbsp;&nbsp;Additionally, the lease has a put option pursuant
to which SHC may require Reading to purchase all or a portion of
SHC’s interest in the existing cinema lease and the cinema ground
lease at any time between July&nbsp;1, 2013 and December&nbsp;4,
2019.&nbsp;&nbsp;SHC’s put option may be exercised on one or more
occasions in increments of not less than $100,000
each.&nbsp;&nbsp;We recorded the Village East Cinema building as a
property asset of $4.7&nbsp;million on our balance sheet based on
the cost carry-over basis from an entity under common control with
a corresponding capital lease liability of $5.9&nbsp;million
presented under other liabilities (see our disclosure in our Annual
Report on Form 10-K filed on March&nbsp;16, 2018, under Part II –
Item 8 (Financial Statements and Supplementary Data) Note 11 –
</font> <font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">Pension
and Other Liabilities</font><font style=
"display: inline;">).</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">In February 2015, we entered into an
amendment of our management agreement with SHP with respect to the
Cinemas 1, 2, 3, increasing our historic management fee (5% of
gross income) to include a return on $750,000 (the “Renovation
Funding Amount”) used principally to purchase and install certain
furniture, fixtures and equipment at the Cinemas 1 ,2,
3.&nbsp;&nbsp; Under the amendment our management fee was increased
to include an amount equivalent to 100% of any incremental positive
cash flow over the average annual positive cash flow over the
three-year period ended December&nbsp;31, 2014 (not to exceed a
cumulative aggregate amount equal to the Renovation Funding Amount)
plus a 15% annual cash-on-cash return on the balance outstanding
form time to time of the Renovation Funding Amount.&nbsp;&nbsp; We
retain ownership of the furniture, fixtures and equipment and have
the right but not the obligation to remove such furniture, fixtures
and equipment (at our own cost and expense) upon the termination of
the management agreement. &nbsp;&nbsp;Our management fees for 2017,
2016 and 2015 were $158,000, $177,000 and
$153,000.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M443" id="_DV_M443"></a><a name="_DV_M444" id=
"_DV_M444"></a><font style="display: inline;">On August&nbsp;31,
2016, SHP secured a new three-year mortgage loan
($20.0&nbsp;million) with Valley National Bank, the proceeds of
which were used to repay the mortgage on the property with the Bank
of Santander ($15.0&nbsp;million), to repay our Company for its
$2.9&nbsp;million loan to SHP, and for working capital
purposes.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M445" id="_DV_M445"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">26</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">OBI Management
Agreement</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M446" id="_DV_M446"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Pursuant to a Theater Management
Agreement (the “Management Agreement”), our live theater operations
were, until 2016, managed by Off-Broadway Investments, LLC (“OBI
Management”), which is wholly owned by Ms.&nbsp;Margaret Cotter who
is the daughter of the late Mr.&nbsp;James J. Cotter, Sr., the
sister of Ellen Cotter and James Cotter, Jr., and a member of our
Board of Directors. That Management Agreement was terminated
effective March&nbsp;10, 2016 in connection with the retention by
our Company of Margaret Cotter as a full time employee.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M447" id="_DV_M447"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">The Theater Management Agreement
generally provided for the payment of a combination of fixed and
incentive fees for the management of our four live
theaters.&nbsp;&nbsp;Historically, these fees have equated to
approximately 21% of the net cash flow generated by these
properties. The fees to be paid to OBI for 2016 and 2015
were</font> <a name="_DV_C243" id="_DV_C243"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$</font><a name="_DV_M448"
id="_DV_M448"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">79,000 and</font> <a name=
"_DV_C244" id="_DV_C244"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$</font><a name="_DV_M449"
id="_DV_M449"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">589,000,
respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;We also reimbursed OBI for certain travel
expenses, shared the cost of an administrative assistant and
provided office space at our New York offices.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
increase in the payment to OBI for 2015 was attributable to work
done by Margaret Cotter, working through OBI, with respect to the
development of our Union Square and Cinemas 1, 2, 3
properties.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M450" id="_DV_M450"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">OBI Management historically
conducted its operations from our office facilities on a rent-free
basis, and we shared the cost of one administrative employee of OBI
Management. We reimbursed travel related expenses for OBI
Management personnel with respect to travel between New York City
and Chicago in connection with the management of the Royal George
complex. Other than these expenses, OBI Management was responsible
for all of its costs and expenses related to the performance of its
management functions.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Management Agreement renewed
automatically each year unless either party gives at least six
months’ prior notice of its determination to allow the Management
Agreement to expire.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, we could terminate the
Management Agreement at any time for cause.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 13.2pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M451" id="_DV_M451"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Effective March&nbsp;10, 2016,
Margaret Cotter became a full time employee of the Company and the
Management Agreement was terminated.&nbsp;&nbsp;As Executive
Vice-President Real Estate Management and Development - NYC,
Ms.&nbsp;Cotter continues to be responsible for the management of
our live theater assets, continues her role heading up the
pre-redevelopment of our New York properties and is our senior
executive responsible for the redevelopment of our New York
properties.&nbsp;&nbsp;Pursuant to the termination agreement,
Ms.&nbsp;Cotter gave up any right she might otherwise have, through
OBI, to income from STOMP.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 11pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M452" id="_DV_M452"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Ms.&nbsp;Cotter's compensation as
Executive Vice-President was recommended by the Compensation
Committee as part of an extensive review of our Company’s overall
executive compensation and approved by the Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;For
2016, Ms.&nbsp;Cotter's base salary was $350,000 ($285,343 being
paid in 2016, reflecting her March&nbsp;10, 2016 start date), and
bonus was $95,000, she was granted a long term incentive of a stock
option for 19,921 shares of Class A common stock and 4,184
restricted stock units under the Company's 2010 Stock Incentive
Plan, as amended, which long term incentives vest over a four year
period.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M453" id="_DV_M453"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Live Theater Play
Investment</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M454" id="_DV_M454"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">From time to time, our officers and Directors
may invest in plays that lease our live theaters.&nbsp;&nbsp;The
play STOMP has been playing in our Orpheum Theatre since prior to
the time we acquired the theater in 2001.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Cotter
Estate and Mr.&nbsp;Michael Forman own an</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">approximately</font> <font style=
"display: inline;">5% interest in that play, an interest that they
have held since prior to our acquisition of the theater. Refer to
our Annual Report on Form 10-K filed on March&nbsp;16, 2018, Item 3
–</font> <font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">Legal
Proceedings</font> <font style="display: inline;">for more
information about the show STOMP.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M455" id="_DV_M455"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Shadow View Land and Farming,
LLC</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M456" id="_DV_M456"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">During 2012, Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Sr., our former
Chair, Chief Executive Officer and controlling stockholder,
contributed $2.5&nbsp;million of cash and $255,000 of his 2011
bonus as his 50% share of the purchase price of an approximately
202 acre parcel of undeveloped land in Coachella, California and to
cover his 50% share of certain costs associated with that
acquisition.&nbsp;&nbsp;This land is held in Shadow View Land and
Farming, LLC (“Shadow View”), which is owned 50% by our Company,
and which is accounted for as a consolidated subsidiary of our
Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;The other 50% interest in Shadow View is owned
by the the Cotter Estate.&nbsp;&nbsp;We are the managing member of
Shadow View, with oversight provided by our Audit and Conflicts
Committee.&nbsp;&nbsp; These services are provided without
compensation.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">As managing member we have from time
to time made capital contributions to Shadow View and have funded
on an interim basis certain operating and other costs. &nbsp;Our
capital contributions have been matched by the Cotter Estate, and
the Cotter Estate has, upon billing, paid its 50% share of all such
interim costs.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">We are advised that Director Guy
Adams historically has performed certain consulting services for
Mr.&nbsp;Cotter, Sr., with respect to Mr.&nbsp;Cotter’s investment
in Shadow View, for which he received a 5% carried interest in any
profits realized by the Cotter Estate calculated after recovery of
the Cotter Estate’s investment in Shadow View plus a 100% return
thereon.&nbsp;&nbsp; To date, no profits have been realized by
Shadow View and, we are advised, no consulting fees have been paid
by the Cotter Estate with respect to Mr.&nbsp;Adam’s historic
consulting services.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M457" id="_DV_M457"></a><a name="_DV_M458" id=
"_DV_M458"></a><a name="_DV_M459" id="_DV_M459"></a><a name=
"_Toc447217859" id="_Toc447217859"></a></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;text-align:center;line-height:100%;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;">27</font></p>
</div>
<hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center" />
<p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p>
<div style="width:100%">
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
&nbsp;</p>
</div>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt">
<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Review, Approval or
Ratification of Transactions with Related Persons</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M460" id="_DV_M460"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The Audit Committee has adopted a written
charter, which includes responsibility for approval of “Related
Party Transactions.”&nbsp;&nbsp;Under its charter, the Audit
Committee performs the functions of the “Conflicts Committee” of
the Board and is delegated responsibility and authority by the
Board to review, consider and negotiate, and to approve or
disapprove on behalf of the Company the terms and conditions of any
and all Related Party Transactions (defined below) with the same
effect as though such actions had been taken by the full
Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any such matter requires no further action by the
Board in order to be binding upon the Company, except in the case
of matters that, under applicable Nevada law, cannot be delegated
to a committee of the Board and must be determined by the full
Board.&nbsp;&nbsp;In those cases where the authority of the Board
cannot be delegated, the Audit Committee nevertheless provides its
recommendation to the full Board.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M461" id="_DV_M461"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">As used in the Audit Committee’s Charter, the
term “Related Party Transaction” means any transaction or
arrangement between the Company on one hand, and on the other hand
(i) any one or more directors, executive officers or stockholders
holding more than 10% of the voting power of the Company (or any
spouse, parent, sibling or heir of any such individual), or (ii)
any one or more entities under common control with any one of such
persons, or (iii) any entity in which one or more such persons
holds more than a 10% interest.&nbsp;&nbsp;Related Party
Transactions do not include matters related to employment or
employee compensation related issues.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M462" id="_DV_M462"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The charter provides that the Audit Committee
reviews transactions subject to the policy and determines whether
or not to approve or ratify those transactions.&nbsp;&nbsp;In doing
so, the Audit Committee takes into account, among other factors it
deems appropriate:</font></p>
<div style="width:100%">
<table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0"

<font style=

<a name="_DV_M463" id="_DV_M463"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">the approximate dollar value of
the amount involved in the transaction and whether the transaction
is material to us;</font></p>

the transaction or the Related Person in the context of the
proposed transaction that would be material to investors in light
of the circumstances of the particular transaction.</font></p>

<a name="_DV_M470" id="_DV_M470"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Director
Independence</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M471" id="_DV_M471"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Our Company common stock is traded
on</font> <a name="_DV_C246" id="_DV_C246"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">NASDAQ</font><a name="_DV_M472"
id="_DV_M472"></a><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">,
and we comply with applicable listing rules of the NASDAQ Stock
Market (the “NASDAQ Listing Rules”). In determining who is an 
“independent director”, we follow the definition in section
5605(a)(2) of the NASDAQ Listing Rules.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M473" id="_DV_M473"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Under such rules, our Board has
determined that the following directors are independent: Guy Adams,
Dr.&nbsp;Judy Codding, William Gould, Edward Kane, Douglas
McEachern and Michael Wrotniak.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M477" id="_DV_M477"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">We are not aware of any applicable
transactions, relationships or arrangements not disclosed above
that were considered by our Board of Directors under the applicable
independence definitions in determining that any of our directors
is independent.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M478" id="_DV_M478"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">Because we are a “controlled
company” under</font> <a name="_DV_C249" id=
"_DV_C249"></a><font style=
"font-weight:bold;color:#0000FF;display: inline;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">NASDAQ
rules</font><a name="_DV_M479" id="_DV_M479"></a><font style=
"display: inline;color:#000000;">, we are not required to and do
not maintain a standing Nominating Committee.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M480" id="_DV_M480"></a><font style=

definition under section 5605(a)(2) of the NASDAQ Listing Rules, we

Cotter, Jr.</font> <a name="_DV_M481" id="_DV_M481"></a><a name=

<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">–
&nbsp;</font><font style=

Accounting Fees and Services</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M486" id="_DV_M486"></a><a name="_Toc447217896" id=
"_Toc447217896"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Summary of Principal Accounting
Fees for Professional Services Rendered</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M487" id="_DV_M487"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Below is a description of the amounts we paid to
Grant Thornton LLP, our independent registered public accountants
for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017.&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M488" id="_DV_M488"></a><a name="_Toc447217897" id=
"_Toc447217897"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Audit Fees</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M489" id="_DV_M489"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">The aggregate fees for professional services for
the audit of our financial statements, audit of internal controls
related to the Sarbanes-Oxley Act, and the reviews of the financial
statements included in our Form 10-K and Form 10-Q provided by
Grant Thornton LLP for 2017 and 2016 were approximately $840,308
and $776,500, respectively.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M490" id="_DV_M490"></a><a name="_Toc447217898" id=
"_Toc447217898"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Audit-Related Fees</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M491" id="_DV_M491"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Grant Thornton LLP did not provide us any audit
related services for 2017 or 2016.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M492" id="_DV_M492"></a><a name="_Toc447217899" id=
"_Toc447217899"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Tax Fees</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M493" id="_DV_M493"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Grant Thornton LLP did not provide us any
products or any services for tax compliance, tax advice, or tax
planning for 2017 or 2016, other than certain tax reasearch, for
which they were paid fees totaling $12,000.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M494" id="_DV_M494"></a><a name="_Toc447217900" id=
"_Toc447217900"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">All Other Fees</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M495" id="_DV_M495"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Grant Thornton LLP did not provide us any
services for 2017 or 2016, other than as set forth
above.</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:10pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M496" id="_DV_M496"></a><a name="_Toc447217901" id=
"_Toc447217901"></a><font style=
"display: inline;font-weight:bold;">Pre-Approval Policies and
Procedures</font></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt 0pt 10pt;text-indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
<a name="_DV_M497" id="_DV_M497"></a><font style=
"display: inline;">Our Audit Committee must pre-approve, to the
extent required by applicable law, all audit services and
permissible non-audit services provided by our independent
registered public accounting firm, except for any</font>
<font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">de minimis</font>
<font style="display: inline;">non-audit
services.&nbsp;&nbsp;Non-audit services are considered</font>
<font style="display: inline;font-style:italic;">de minimis</font>
<font style="display: inline;">if (i) the aggregate amount of all
such non-audit services constitutes less than 5% of the total
amount of revenues we paid to our independent registered public
accounting firm during the fiscal year in which they are provided;
(ii) we did not recognize such services at the time of the
engagement to be non-audit services; and (iii) such services are
promptly submitted to our Audit Committee for approval prior to the
completion of the audit by our Audit Committee or any of its
members who has authority to give such approval.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our
Audit Committee pre-approved all services provided to us by Grant
Thornton LLP for 2017 and 2016.</font><a name="_DV_X0" id=
"_DV_X0"></a></p>
<p style=
"margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
